TRIPS :   1379 REPORT TOTAL :                  0.000 18042.019       019122653.00  3718535.00   953300.00     8454759.00  74600.00  8529359.00

DO setout WITH "Balance Payment Detail"
headpnm= "pghead"
footpnm= "footer"
endpnm = "resetrepo"
IF !outdev()
	RETU .F.
ENDIF
msdate = _sdate
medate=IIF(BETW(DATE(), _sdate, _edate), DATE(), _edate)
IF getdates(-1, .T.)
	tmsdate = msdate
	tmedate = medate
	msdate = _sdate
	medate=IIF(BETW(DATE(), _sdate, _edate), DATE(), _edate)
	IF getdates(-1, .T.)
		@ 4, 7 SAY "Vehicle Type   :" GET destype DEFAULT " " PICTURE "@!" MESSAGE "Leave Blank for All"
		READ
		CLEAR
		IF MOD(READ(),256) != 12
			IF ophelp("company.name", "company.code", "-Ocompname-P")
				IF ophelp("area.name", "-Oareaname-P")
					IF setrepo()
						heading = heading()
						DO pghead
						DO printrep
						DO lastfoot
					ENDIF
				ENDIF
			ENDIF
		ENDIF
	ENDIF
ENDIF
DO resetout
RETU .T.

FUNC setrepo
SET ORDER TO areacode IN area
SET ORDER TO compcode IN company
wcond = IIF(EMPT(destype), " .T. ", " s.ownveh = destype ")

	SELE s.vehno, s.tfreight, s.advance, s.cadvance, s.a_cheque, s.a_bank, s.vno, s.balance, s.tdsamt, ;
	 s.unload+s.detaintion+s.epoint+s.chanda+s.other-s.shortage AS other, ;
	 s.bank, s.cheque, s.chqdate, s.b_name, ;
	 s.odate, s.ovno, s.narration, sd.* ;
	FROM bill s, billdet sd, company p, area a ;
	WHERE s.invno=sd.invno AND BETW(s.idate,msdate,medate) AND ;
		BETW(s.odate,tmsdate,tmedate) AND ;
		sd.company=p.code AND p.consider AND &wcond AND sd.area=a.code AND a.consider ;
	ORDER BY s.idate, sd.invno, s.vehno ;
	INTO TABLE desreg
SELE desreg
SET RELA TO area INTO area, company INTO company
GO TOP
RETU !EOF()

FUNC resetrepo
=closedbf("desreg", "-")
RETU .T.

FUNC heading
retdata = "Date  Vehicle No      Destination               Wt   Case Truck Fr  Cash Ad.  Chq Adv Balance   Other  Ac.Bl.Pd Bal.P.Dt Chq No.  Bank"
RETU retdata

FUNC pghead
?_company
?REPL("_",80)
?"BALANCE PAYMENT DETAIL FOR "
??IIF(destype=" ", "ALL VEHICLES", IIF(destype="O", "OWN VEHICLES", IIF(destype="H", "HIRED VEHICLES", "")))
?"PERIOD", msdate, "TO", medate, "FOR", tmsdate, "TO", tmedate, ""
?
?heading
?REPL("-",LEN(heading))
?
RETU .T.

FUNC printrep
GO TOP
STORE 0 TO rwt, rotherwt, rqty, rfr, rtfr, radv, rqadv, rbal, roth, rabp, trips
DO WHILE !EOF()
	STORE 0 TO twt, totherwt, tqty, tfr
	STORE "" TO tarea
	grp1 = DTOS(idate)+invno
	DO WHILE grp1 = DTOS(idate)+invno AND !EOF()
		IF !(ALLT(area.name) $ tarea)
			tarea = tarea + ALLT(area.name)
			tarea = tarea + IIF(company="OC", "-"+ALLT(no), "")
			tarea = tarea + "| "
		ENDIF
		IF company="PP"
			twt = twt + weight
			tqty = tqty + qty
		ELSE
			totherwt = totherwt + weight
		ENDIF
		tfr = tfr + freight
		SKIP
	ENDDO
		?LEFT(DTOC(idate),5), vehno, tarea, twt PICT "@Z 9999.999", totherwt PICT "@Z 9999.999", tqty PICT "@Z 999999",
		  tfreight PICT "999999.99", advance PICT "99999.99", ;
		  cadvance PICT "99999.99", ;
		  balance-tdsamt PICT "99999.99", tother PICT "99999.99", ;
		  balance+tother-tdsamt PICT "99999.99", ;
		  IIF(EMPT(odate), "", y2k(odate)), PADL(ALLT(a_cheque),10), ALLT(a_bank), 
		  LEFT(bank,10), LEFT(ALLT(cheque),11), IIF(EMPT(chqdate), "", chqdate), ALLT(b_name)
		rwt = rwt + twt
		rotherwt = rotherwt + totherwt
		rqty = rqty + tqty
		rfr = rfr + tfr
		rtfr = rtfr + tfreight
		radv = radv + advance
		rqadv = rqadv + cadvance
		rbal = rbal + balance - tdsamt
		roth = roth + tother
		rabp = rabp + (balance+tother-tdsamt)
		trips = trips + 1
ENDDO
?"TRIPS :", trips PICT "999999", "REPORT TOTAL :", rwt PICT "99999.999" AT 43, rotherwt PICT "99999.999", rqty PICT "9999999",
rtfr PICT "99999999.99", radv PICT "99999999.99", rqadv PICT "99999999.99", rbal PICT "99999999999.99", roth PICT "999999.99", rabp PICT "99999999.99"
RETU .T.
